--High Distinction Spring 2018
--Paul Jiang Paul.jiang@student.uts.edu.au
--Stock Market database allowing users to analysis the performance of any company in the top 200
--and different sectors (for example energy, materials and etc)
--ABOUT
--GICS (Global Industry Classification Standard) is jointly developed by S&P Dow Jones Indices 
--and MSCI aimed at standardising global industry definitions. GICS provides us tools to to compare companies of 
--similar operations. The more specialised the category is the better the comparison. 
--For example a comparison between BHP (Mining Co) and CBA (Bank) is not as fair as comparing CBA to NAB (Bank)
--Using data from history and outstanding tables we can identify the best performing company it is classification
--
--In Australia we can trade shares (a partial ownership in a company) for money. A person can have multiple 
--different shares in different company and a company can trade with any one person. The records of transactions
--between a person and a company is recorded in the transaction table
--
--List is used to help us to create plans. A transaction can be record against a list, for example we want 
--to develop a plan to invest in the short term and in the long term. In the short term we could have transaction
--with BHP, however in the long term list we CBA and NAB. List also have master list for hierarchical organisation

DROP VIEW daily_return CASCADE;
DROP VIEW capital_market CASCADE;
DROP VIEW banks_market CASCADE;
DROP VIEW energy_company CASCADE;
DROP VIEW energy_market CASCADE;
DROP VIEW materials_company CASCADE;
DROP VIEW materials_market CASCADE;
DROP VIEW industrials_company CASCADE;
DROP VIEW industrials_market CASCADE;
DROP VIEW Consumer_Discretionary_company CASCADE;
DROP VIEW Consumer_Discretionary_market CASCADE;
DROP VIEW Consumer_Staples_company CASCADE;
DROP VIEW Consumer_Staples_market CASCADE;
DROP VIEW Health_Care_company CASCADE;
DROP VIEW Health_Care_market CASCADE;
DROP VIEW financials_company CASCADE;

DROP VIEW IT_company CASCADE;
DROP VIEW IT_market CASCADE;
DROP VIEW Communication_Services_company CASCADE;

DROP VIEW Utilities_company CASCADE;
DROP VIEW Utilities_market CASCADE;
DROP VIEW real_estate_company CASCADE;
DROP VIEW real_estate_market CASCADE;

DROP TABLE transactions;
DROP TABLE person CASCADE;
DROP TABLE list CASCADE;
DROP TABLE outstandingShares CASCADE;
DROP TABLE history CASCADE;
DROP TABLE company CASCADE;
DROP TABLE subIndustry;
DROP TABLE Industry CASCADE;
DROP TABLE Sector CASCADE;


CREATE TABLE Sector (
	sectorID	INTEGER,
	sectorName	TEXT UNIQUE,
	CONSTRAINT sector_pk PRIMARY KEY (sectorID)
);


CREATE TABLE Industry (
	industryID	INTEGER,
	industryName	TEXT UNIQUE,
	sectorID	INTEGER NOT NULL,
	CONSTRAINT industry_pk PRIMARY KEY (industryID),
	CONSTRAINT industry_fk FOREIGN KEY (sectorID) REFERENCES Sector ON DELETE CASCADE
);


CREATE TABLE subIndustry (
	subIndustryID	INTEGER,
	subIndustryName	TEXT UNIQUE,
	industryID	INTEGER NOT NULL,
	CONSTRAINT subIndustry_pk PRIMARY KEY (subIndustryID),
	CONSTRAINT subIndustry_fk FOREIGN KEY (industryID) REFERENCES Industry ON DELETE CASCADE
);

CREATE TABLE company (
	companyCode	CHAR(3),
	companyName	TEXT UNIQUE,
	subIndustryID	INTEGER NOT NULL,
	CONSTRAINT company_pk PRIMARY KEY (companyCode),
	CONSTRAINT company_pf FOREIGN KEY (subIndustryID) REFERENCES subIndustry ON DELETE RESTRICT
);
CREATE TABLE outstandingShares (
	companyCode	CHAR(3),
	MVdate		DATE NOT NULL,
	outstanding	BIGINT,
	CONSTRAINT outstandingShares_pk PRIMARY KEY (companyCode, MVdate),
	CONSTRAINT outstandingShares_fk FOREIGN KEY (companyCode) REFERENCES company ON DELETE CASCADE,
	CONSTRAINT valid_outstanding CHECK (outstanding > 0)
);
CREATE TABLE history (
	companyCode	CHAR(3),
	HSdate		TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
	openPrice	DECIMAL(5,2),
	high		DECIMAL(5,2),
	low		DECIMAL(5,2),
	closePrice 	DECIMAL(5,2),
	tradeVolume	BIGINT,
	CONSTRAINT history_pk PRIMARY KEY (companyCode, HSdate),
	CONSTRAINT history_fk FOREIGN KEY (companyCode) REFERENCES company ON DELETE CASCADE,
	CONSTRAINT allowed_values CHECK (
		high > low AND 
		low < high AND 
		openprice > 0 AND 
		high > 0 AND 
		low > 0 AND 
		closeprice > 0 AND 
		tradeVolume > 0),
	CONSTRAINT valid_hsdate CHECK 
		((HSdate::time >= '10:00' AND HSdate::time <= '16:12') AND 
		(date_part('dow', HSdate) <> 6 OR date_part('dow', HSdate) <> 7))
);
CREATE TABLE person (
	personID	SERIAL,
	firstname 	VARCHAR(20),
	lastname	VARCHAR(20),
	balance		DECIMAL(10,2),
	description	TEXT,
	CONSTRAINT person_pk PRIMARY KEY (personID),
	CONSTRAINT positive_balance CHECK (balance > 0)
);
CREATE TABLE list (
	listcode	VARCHAR(10),
	listname	TEXT,
	parentcode	VARCHAR(10) DEFAULT NULL,
	CONSTRAINT listname_pk PRIMARY KEY (listcode),
	CONSTRAINT parentlist_fk FOREIGN KEY (parentcode) REFERENCES list ON DELETE CASCADE
);
-- note that there is no need for a matching PK to FK 
-- note that not all transaction will be linked to a list, therefore optional
CREATE TABLE transactions (
	companyCode	CHAR(3),
	personID	INTEGER,
	transDate	TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
	listcode	VARCHAR(10),
	CONSTRAINT transaction_pk PRIMARY KEY (companyCode, personID, transDate),
	CONSTRAINT transaction_company_fk FOREIGN KEY (companyCode) REFERENCES company ON DELETE NO ACTION,
	CONSTRAINT transaction_person_fk FOREIGN KEY (personID) REFERENCES person ON DELETE CASCADE,
	CONSTRAINT transaction_list_fk FOREIGN KEY (listcode) REFERENCES list ON DELETE SET NULL
	CONSTRAINT valid_transdate CHECK 
		((transdate::time >= '10:00' AND transdate::time <= '16:12') AND 
		(date_part('dow',transdate) <> 6 OR date_part('dow', transdate) <> 7))
);
CREATE VIEW daily_return AS
SELECT 	one.companycode, one.hsdate::date,
	((one.closeprice - two.closeprice)/ two.closeprice*100):: DECIMAL(4,2) AS daily_yield 
FROM history one, history two 
WHERE one.companycode = two.companycode 
AND one.hsdate::date = two.hsdate::date + 
	CASE WHEN DATE_PART('dow',one.hsdate) = 1 THEN 
	3 ELSE 
	1 END;

CREATE VIEW capital_market AS
SELECT hsdate::date, sum(closeprice*outstanding) As MarketValue 
FROM history NATURAL JOIN company NATURAL JOIN outstandingshares 
WHERE subindustryid = ANY 
	(SELECT subindustryid FROM subindustry NATURAL JOIN industry 
	WHERE industryname = 'Capital Markets') 
GROUP BY hsdate 
ORDER BY hsdate; 

CREATE VIEW banks_market AS
SELECT hsdate::date, sum(closeprice*outstanding) As MarketValue 
FROM history NATURAL JOIN company NATURAL JOIN outstandingshares 
WHERE subindustryid = ANY 
	(SELECT subindustryid FROM subindustry NATURAL JOIN industry 
	WHERE industryname = 'Banks') 
GROUP BY hsdate 
ORDER BY hsdate; 


CREATE VIEW energy_company AS
SELECT companycode, hsdate::date, closeprice*outstanding AS MarketValue FROM history NATURAL JOIN company NATURAL JOIN outstandingshares
WHERE subindustryid = ANY (
	SELECT subindustryid 
	FROM subindustry NATURAL JOIN industry NATURAL JOIN sector
	WHERE sectorname = 'Energy')
ORDER BY hsdate, companycode;

	WHERE sectorname = 'Materials')
